---

# OpenSpec Architecture — Structured Summary

## 1. Overall Architecture Layers

The system is organized into four conceptual layers:

| Layer | Description | Key Modules |
|---|---|---|
| **1. CLI / Command Layer** | User-facing commands that orchestrate workflows | `init.ts`, `update.ts`, `archive.ts`, `list.ts`, `specs-apply.ts` |
| **2. Core Domain Logic** | The artifact graph engine, change lifecycle, workspaces, and collections | `artifact-graph/`, `change-metadata/`, `collections/`, `planning-home.ts` |
| **3. Configuration System** | Global, project, and schema configuration with validation | `global-config.ts`, `project-config.ts`, `config-schema.ts`, `config-prompts.ts` |
| **4. Tool Integration Layer** | AI-tool-specific command generation and adapter system | `command-generation/`, `available-tools.ts`, `config.ts` |

---

## 2. Core Modules and Their Responsibilities

### 2.1 Artifact Graph (`src/core/artifact-graph/`)

The central engine that models **workflow schemas as directed acyclic graphs (DAGs)**.

| File | Responsibility |
|---|---|
| `types.ts` | Zod schemas for `Artifact`, `ApplyPhase`, `SchemaYaml`; runtime types `CompletedSet`, `BlockedArtifacts` |
| `schema.ts` | Parse YAML → validate with Zod → run semantic checks (no dups, valid refs, no cycles) |
| `graph.ts` | `ArtifactGraph` class: topological sort (Kahn's algorithm), `getNextArtifacts`, `getBlocked`, `isComplete` |
| `state.ts` | `detectCompleted()` — scans filesystem for artifact output files to determine completion |
| `resolver.ts` | Schema resolution: project-local → user override → package built-in (3-tier override chain) |
| `outputs.ts` | Resolve artifact output paths (supports glob patterns), check file existence |
| `instruction-loader.ts` | `loadChangeContext()`, `generateInstructions()`, `formatChangeStatus()` — bridges graph state to AI instructions |
| `index.ts` | Public barrel exports |

### 2.2 Change Metadata (`src/core/change-metadata/`)

| File | Responsibility |
|---|---|
| `schema.ts` | Zod schema for per-change metadata (`ChangeMetadata`): schema name, creation date, goal, affected_areas, initiative link |
| `index.ts` | Barrel export |

### 2.3 Collections / Initiatives (`src/core/collections/`)

A **generic collection framework** for mounting data stores, with **initiatives** as the primary concrete collection.

| File | Responsibility |
|---|---|
| `runtime.ts` | Generic `CollectionRegistry`, `MountedCollection`, `mountCollections()` — abstract collection mounting system |
| `initiatives/schema.ts` | Initiative state schema: id, title, summary, status (exploring/active/complete/archived), owners, metadata; file name constants |
| `initiatives/collection.ts` | `createInitiativesCollectionRegistry()`, `mountInitiativesCollection()` — wires initiatives into the collection system |
| `initiatives/operations.ts` | CRUD operations: `createInitiative`, `listInitiatives`, `readInitiative`, `archiveInitiative` |
| `initiatives/resolution.ts` | `resolveInitiativeReference()` — resolves initiative links across context stores with diagnostics |
| `initiatives/templates.ts` | Default Markdown templates for requirements, design, decisions, questions, tasks |

### 2.4 Planning Home (`src/core/planning-home.ts`)

Resolves the **"planning home"** — the root directory that owns a change's planning artifacts. Supports two modes:
- **`repo` mode**: finds nearest ancestor with `openspec/` directory
- **`workspace` mode**: finds nearest ancestor with a workspace state file

### 2.5 Configuration System

| File | Responsibility |
|---|---|
| `global-config.ts` | XDG-based global config (`~/.config/openspec/config.json`): profile, delivery mode, feature flags, workflows |
| `project-config.ts` | Per-project config (`openspec/config.yaml`): schema name, context, per-artifact rules |
| `config-schema.ts` | Zod schema for global config validation |
| `config-prompts.ts` | `serializeConfig()` — generates commented YAML for new projects |

### 2.6 Profiles (`src/core/profiles.ts`)

Defines **workflow profiles**:
- **`core`**: 5 workflows — propose, explore, apply, sync, archive
- **`custom`**: user-selected subset of all 11 available workflows

### 2.7 CLI Commands

| File | Command | Purpose |
|---|---|---|
| `init.ts` | `openspec init` | One-time project setup: installs Agent Skills + `/opsx:*` slash commands for configured AI tools |
| `update.ts` | `openspec update` | Refreshes skills/commands, detects profile/delivery drift, handles migration |
| `archive.ts` | `openspec archive` | Archives a change: validates specs, applies delta specs to main specs, moves change to archive |
| `list.ts` | `openspec list` | Lists changes or specs with completion status, sorting, JSON output |
| `specs-apply.ts` | (used by archive) | Applies delta specs from a change to main specs (find → build → write) |

### 2.8 Change Status Policy (`src/core/change-status-policy.ts`)

Provides **context-aware decision logic** for the change workflow:
- `buildActionContext()` — determines mode (repo-local vs workspace-planning), edit roots, constraints
- `summarizeAffectedAreas()` — validates affected areas against workspace links
- `buildNextSteps()` — generates plain-language next steps based on artifact statuses

### 2.9 Command Generation System (`src/core/command-generation/`)

A **pluggable adapter system** for generating AI-tool-specific command files.

| File | Responsibility |
|---|---|
| `types.ts` | `CommandContent` (tool-agnostic), `ToolCommandAdapter` (interface), `GeneratedCommand` |
| `registry.ts` | `CommandAdapterRegistry` — static registry of 25+ tool adapters |
| `generator.ts` | `generateCommand()` / `generateCommands()` — generic file generation |
| `index.ts` | Barrel exports |

### 2.10 Tool Detection (`src/core/available-tools.ts`)

`getAvailableTools()` — scans project root for AI tool config directories (`.claude/`, `.cursor/`, etc.) to auto-detect which tools are in use.

### 2.11 Profile Sync Drift (`src/core/profile-sync-drift.ts`)

`hasToolProfileOrDeliveryDrift()` — detects when installed skills/commands don't match the desired profile and delivery mode, enabling `openspec update` to fix inconsistencies.

---

## 3. Key Data Flow (How Artifacts Flow Through the System)

```
Schema YAML (on disk)
    │
    ▼
parseSchema() ──► SchemaYaml (validated Zod object)
    │
    ▼
ArtifactGraph.fromSchema() ──► ArtifactGraph (DAG with Map<id, Artifact>)
    │
    ▼
loadChangeContext() ──► ChangeContext { graph, completed, metadata, ... }
    │                        │
    │                        ▼
    │              detectCompleted() ──► CompletedSet
    │                        │          (filesystem scan)
    │                        ▼
    │              formatChangeStatus() ──► ChangeStatus
    │                        │          (status, nextSteps, actionContext)
    │                        ▼
    ▼              AI receives enriched instructions
generateInstructions() ──► ArtifactInstructions
    │                        │
    │                        ├── template (from schema/templates/)
    │                        ├── context (from project config)
    │                        ├── rules (from project config)
    │                        ├── dependency info
    │                        └── output paths
    ▼
AI writes artifact files → filesystem
    │
    ▼
detectCompleted() picks up new files → cycle continues
```

**Artifact lifecycle within a single change:**
1. Schema defines artifacts with `requires` (dependencies)
2. `getNextArtifacts()` returns artifacts whose deps are all done
3. AI creates each artifact → file written to disk
4. `detectCompleted()` scans files → updates `CompletedSet`
5. `getBlocked()` shows artifacts still waiting on deps
6. When all artifacts done → `isComplete()` = true → apply phase available

---

## 4. Module Dependency Relationships

```
src/core/index.ts
  ├── global-config.ts          (standalone)
  ├── workspace/index.ts        (standalone)
  ├── context-store/index.ts    (standalone)
  ├── collections/index.ts
  │     ├── runtime.ts          (standalone)
  │     └── initiatives/
  │           ├── schema.ts     (standalone)
  │           ├── collection.ts → runtime.ts
  │           ├── operations.ts → schema.ts, templates.ts, collection.ts
  │           ├── resolution.ts → collection.ts, operations.ts, context-store/
  │           └── templates.ts  → schema.ts
  ├── planning-home.ts          → workspace/
  ├── change-metadata/
  │     └── schema.ts           (standalone, Zod only)
  ├── artifact-graph/
  │     ├── types.ts            (standalone, Zod only)
  │     ├── schema.ts           → types.ts
  │     ├── graph.ts            → types.ts, schema.ts
  │     ├── state.ts            → types.ts, graph.ts, outputs.ts
  │     ├── resolver.ts         → schema.ts, global-config.ts
  │     ├── outputs.ts          (standalone, fast-glob)
  │     ├── instruction-loader.ts → graph.ts, state.ts, resolver.ts, outputs.ts,
  │     │                          change-metadata/, project-config.ts,
  │     │                          change-status-policy.ts
  │     └── index.ts            (barrel)
  ├── change-status-policy.ts   → change-metadata/, planning-home.ts
  ├── project-config.ts         (standalone, YAML + Zod)
  ├── config-schema.ts          (standalone, Zod)
  ├── config-prompts.ts         → project-config.ts
  ├── config.ts                 (standalone, AI_TOOLS list)
  ├── available-tools.ts        → config.ts
  ├── profiles.ts               → global-config.ts
  ├── profile-sync-drift.ts     → config.ts, profiles.ts, command-generation/
  ├── command-generation/
  │     ├── types.ts            (standalone)
  │     ├── registry.ts         → types.ts, adapters/*
  │     ├── generator.ts        → types.ts
  │     └── index.ts            (barrel)
  ├── init.ts                   → config.ts, profiles.ts, command-generation/,
  │                                available-tools.ts, global-config.ts, etc.
  ├── update.ts                 → config.ts, profiles.ts, command-generation/,
  │                                available-tools.ts, profile-sync-drift.ts, etc.
  ├── archive.ts                → specs-apply.ts, validation/
  ├── list.ts                   → (standalone, reads filesystem)
  └── specs-apply.ts            → (standalone, reads filesystem)
```

---

## 5. Key Design Patterns Used

| Pattern | Where | How |
|---|---|---|
| **Dependency Graph / DAG** | `artifact-graph/` | Artifacts form a DAG; topological sort (Kahn's algorithm) for build order |
| **Strategy / Adapter** | `command-generation/` | `ToolCommandAdapter` interface with 25+ implementations; `CommandAdapterRegistry` for lookup |
| **Registry** | `command-generation/registry.ts`, `collections/runtime.ts` | Static and dynamic registries for adapters and collections |
| **Filesystem-as-State** | `state.ts`, `outputs.ts` | Completion is detected by checking if artifact output files exist on disk — no database |
| **Three-tier Override Chain** | `resolver.ts` | Schema resolution: project-local → user override → package built-in |
| **Schema-First Validation** | Every schema module | Zod schemas as single source of truth for types + runtime validation |
| **Composition Root** | `instruction-loader.ts` | `loadChangeContext()` composes graph + state + metadata + config into a single context object |
| **Policy Object** | `change-status-policy.ts` | `buildActionContext()` encapsulates workspace/repo policy decisions |
| **Template Method** | `initiatives/templates.ts` | Default templates with structured sections that can be overridden |
| **Builder Pattern** | `generateInstructions()` | Builds enriched `ArtifactInstructions` by composing template + context + rules + deps |

---

## 6. The Artifact Graph Model

### Node (Artifact)
```typescript
interface Artifact {
  id: string;           // Unique identifier (e.g., "proposal", "tasks")
  generates: string;    // Output file pattern (e.g., "proposal.md", "tasks/*.md")
  description: string;  // Human-readable purpose
  template: string;     // Relative path to template file in schema's templates/
  instruction: string;  // Optional custom guidance for AI
  requires: string[];   // IDs of artifacts that must be completed first
}
```

### Edge (Dependency)
- Edges are **implicit** via the `requires` array on each artifact
- Direction: `requires` → artifact (dependency points to prerequisite)
- The graph is validated to have: no duplicate IDs, valid references, no cycles

### States
Each artifact is in one of three states, determined by filesystem scanning:

| State | Meaning | Detection |
|---|---|---|
| **done** | Output file(s) exist on disk | `artifactOutputExists()` — checks file/glob |
| **ready** | All `requires` are done, but own output doesn't exist | `getNextArtifacts()` |
| **blocked** | Some `requires` not yet done | `getBlocked()` returns unmet deps |

### Graph Operations
- **`getBuildOrder()`** — Kahn's algorithm topological sort (deterministic via sorted queue)
- **`getNextArtifacts(completed)`** — artifacts whose deps are all done
- **`getBlocked(completed)`** — artifacts with unmet deps, grouped by artifact
- **`isComplete(completed)`** — all artifacts done

### Apply Phase
The schema can optionally define an `apply` phase:
```typescript
interface ApplyPhase {
  requires: string[];      // Artifacts that must exist before apply
  tracks: string | null;   // Optional checkbox file for progress tracking
  instruction: string;     // Custom guidance for the apply step
}
```

---

## 7. The Change Lifecycle

A **change** is a named directory under `openspec/changes/<change-name>/` that contains planning artifacts.

```
1. PROPOSE ──► 2. EXPLORE ──► 3. NEW/CONTINUE ──► 4. APPLY ──► 5. ARCHIVE
                                                      │
                                                      ▼
                                              specs-apply.ts
                                              (delta → main specs)
```

| Phase | Artifacts Created | Description |
|---|---|---|
| **propose** | `proposal.md` | Define the change scope and goal |
| **explore** | `exploration/` | Investigate options, gather context |
| **new** | Schema-defined artifacts | Create artifacts in a fresh change |
| **continue** | Schema-defined artifacts | Resume work on an existing change |
| **apply** | (specs applied) | Apply delta specs to main specs, validate |
| **archive** | (moved to archive/) | Archive the change directory |

**Metadata** (`openspec.yaml` in each change directory):
```yaml
schema: spec-driven          # Which schema this change uses
created: 2025-01-15          # Creation date
goal: "..."                  # Change goal
affected_areas: ["area1"]    # For workspace-mode changes
initiative:                  # Optional link to shared context
  store: my-store
  id: my-initiative
```

---

## 8. The Initiative / Workspace Model

### Context Store
A **context store** is a directory on disk that hosts collections (mounted subdirectories). The store root is resolved via `resolveSelectedContextStore()`.

### Collections
A generic mounting system:
```typescript
interface CollectionDefinition {
  id: string;       // kebab-case identifier
  mount: string;    // subdirectory name within store
}
```
`mountCollections()` takes a store root + registry, produces `MountedCollection` objects with path resolution and security (path-escape prevention).

### Initiatives (the primary collection)
An **initiative** is a durable unit of shared context stored in a context store:
- Directory per initiative: `<store>/initiatives/<initiative-id>/`
- Contains `initiative.yaml` (state metadata) + up to 5 Markdown files:
  - `requirements.md`, `design.md`, `decisions.md`, `questions.md`, `tasks.md`
- Status lifecycle: `exploring → active → complete | archived`
- Changes can **link** to initiatives via `metadata.initiative = { store, id }`

### Workspace Planning
The **planning home** resolves to either:
- **`repo` mode**: nearest ancestor with `openspec/` directory
- **`workspace` mode**: nearest ancestor with workspace state file

In workspace mode, `buildActionContext()` enforces:
- `sourceOfTruth = 'workspace-local'`
- `requiresAffectedAreaSelection = true`
- `allowedEditRoots = []` (read-only context until explicitly set)

---

## 9. The CLI Command Structure

Commands are invoked via `openspec <command>`:

| Command | Entry Point | Key Behavior |
|---|---|---|
| `init` | `InitCommand.execute()` | Sets up project: writes config, installs Agent Skills + `/opsx:*` slash commands for all detected AI tools |
| `update` | `UpdateCommand.execute()` | Refreshes skills/commands, detects drift, runs migration |
| `archive [name]` | `ArchiveCommand.execute()` | Validates, applies specs, moves to archive |
| `list [changes|specs]` | `ListCommand.execute()` | Lists changes with task completion, sorting, JSON |
| `apply` | (via archive) | `findSpecUpdates()` → `buildUpdatedSpec()` → `writeUpdatedSpec()` |

The `init` command is the most complex, orchestrating:
1. Config file generation (`serializeConfig()`)
2. AI tool detection (`getAvailableTools()`)
3. Profile-based workflow selection (`getProfileWorkflows()`)
4. Skill generation (`generateSkillContent()`) — writes `.md` files to tool skill directories
5. Command generation (`generateCommands()`) — writes `/opsx:*` slash command files via adapters
6. Legacy cleanup (`cleanupLegacyArtifacts()`)

---

## 10. The Command Generation / Adapter System

### Architecture

```
CommandContent (tool-agnostic)
    │
    ▼
ToolCommandAdapter (interface)
    ├── getFilePath(commandId) → path
    └── formatFile(content) → formatted string
    │
    ▼
CommandAdapterRegistry (static)
    ├── register(adapter)
    ├── get(toolId) → adapter
    └── getAll() → adapters[]
    │
    ▼
generateCommands(contents[], adapter) → GeneratedCommand[]
```

### Key Interfaces

```typescript
interface CommandContent {
  id: string;          // e.g., "explore"
  name: string;        // e.g., "OpenSpec Explore"
  description: string; // Brief purpose
  category: string;    // e.g., "Workflow"
  tags: string[];      // e.g., ["openspec", "workflow"]
  body: string;        // The instruction content
}

interface ToolCommandAdapter {
  toolId: string;      // e.g., "claude", "cursor"
  getFilePath(commandId: string): string;  // Where to write the file
  formatFile(content: CommandContent): string;  // How to format (frontmatter, etc.)
}
```

### Adapter Registry

The `CommandAdapterRegistry` is a **static registry** initialized at module load time with 25+ built-in adapters (Claude Code, Cursor, Windsurf, Cline, Gemini CLI, GitHub Copilot, etc.). Each adapter knows:
- The **file path convention** for its tool (e.g., `.claude/commands/opsx/explore.md`)
- The **frontmatter format** (YAML frontmatter, JSON, or tool-specific header syntax)

### Separation of Concerns

The command generation system cleanly separates:
- **What** to generate (`CommandContent` — defined by OpenSpec's workflow needs)
- **How** to format it (`ToolCommandAdapter` — defined by each AI tool's conventions)
- **Where** to put it (`getFilePath()` — defined by each tool's config directory structure)

This allows adding support for a new AI tool by implementing a single adapter class — no changes to the core workflow logic.

---

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
